  <span m='212620'>index</span> <span m='212980'>is</span> <span m='213130'>encoded</span>

  <span m='214360'>byte,</span> <span m='214960'>so</span> <span m='215050'>32-bit</span>
  <span m='215560'>integer,</span> <span m='216950'>which</span> <span m='217060'>is</span>
  <span m='217180'>kind</span> <span m='217360'>of</span> <span m='217450'>overkill,</span>
  <span m='217960'>because</span> <span m='218140'>I</span> <span m='218230'>think</span>
  <span m='218440'>the</span> <span m='218530'>most</span> <span m='218860'>that</span>
  <span m='219010'>there's</span> <span m='219250'>ever--</span> <span m='219945'>the</span>
  <span m='220210'>most</span> <span m='220450'>outputs</span> <span m='220870'>there's</span>
  <span m='221080'>ever</span> <span m='221290'>been</span> <span m='221620'>is</span>
  <span m='221740'>like</span> <span m='221890'>1,000</span> <span m='222370'>or</span>
  <span m='222460'>something.</span> </p><p><span m='223480'>So</span> <span m='223870'>you</span>
  <span m='223990'>really</span> <span m='224380'>don't</span> <span m='224560'>need</span>
  <span m='225180'>it</span> <span m='225280'>to</span> <span m='225400'>be</span>
  <span m='225580'>able</span> <span m='225700'>to</span> <span m='225760'>go</span>
  <span m='225850'>up</span> <span m='225940'>to</span> <span m='226030'>4</span>
  <span m='226190'>billion.</span> <span m='227440'>But</span> <span m='227950'>that's</span>
  <span m='228100'>how</span> <span m='228190'>it</span> <span m='228280'>is.</span>
  </p><p><span m='229450'>The</span> <span m='229570'>signature</span> <span m='229990'>ends</span>

  <span m='241750'>those</span> <span m='241930'>things</span> <span m='242170'>could</span>
  <span m='242320'>be</span> <span m='243220'>much</span> <span m='243460'>more</span>
  <span m='243580'>efficient.</span> <span m='244040'>But</span> <span m='244060'>they're</span>
  <span m='244140'>not</span> <span m='245320'>yet.</span> </p><p><span m='246560'>And</span>
  <span m='246670'>the</span> <span m='246790'>output</span> <span m='247000'>is</span>
  <span m='247090'>actually</span> <span m='247330'>a</span> <span m='247360'>lot</span>
  <span m='247480'>smaller.</span> <span m='248170'>An</span> <span m='248260'>output,</span>

  <span m='284590'>but</span> <span m='284860'>yeah,</span> <span m='285070'>whatever.</span>
  <span m='286180'>So</span> <span m='286600'>this</span> <span m='286920'>ends</span>

  <span m='305680'>is</span> <span m='305800'>the</span> <span m='305890'>mining</span>
  <span m='306250'>process?</span> <span m='307360'>So</span> <span m='307600'>in</span>

  <span m='312280'>last</span> <span m='312520'>block</span> <span m='312760'>was,</span>
  <span m='313450'>put</span> <span m='313630'>your</span> <span m='313720'>name</span>

  <span m='329170'>another.</span> <span m='330820'>They</span> <span m='330940'>make</span>

  <span m='332680'>they</span> <span m='332740'>broadcast.</span> <span m='334240'>I'll</span>
  <span m='334390'>get</span> <span m='334600'>in</span> <span m='334890'>to</span>

  </p><p><span m='336860'>So</span> <span m='337080'>in</span> <span m='337990'>the</span>

  </p><p><span m='357040'>They're</span> <span m='357250'>all</span> <span m='357550'>listening</span>

  <span m='358930'>in.</span> <span m='359180'>They're</span> <span m='359380'>all</span>
  <span m='359470'>connecting</span> <span m='359920'>out</span> <span m='360070'>to</span>

  <span m='363400'>they</span> <span m='363520'>broadcast.</span> <span m='363960'>So</span>
  <span m='364090'>if</span> <span m='364150'>someone</span> <span m='364510'>sends</span>

  <span m='365410'>you'll</span> <span m='366100'>pass</span> <span m='366400'>it</span>
  <span m='366490'>on</span> <span m='366730'>to</span> <span m='366820'>all</span>

  <span m='372850'>fairly</span> <span m='373300'>heavy</span> <span m='373570'>load</span>

  <span m='376780'>sign</span> <span m='377200'>them,</span> <span m='377490'>broadcast</span>
  <span m='377910'>them.</span> <span m='378880'>And</span> <span m='379000'>then</span>

  <span m='388930'>So</span> <span m='389010'>those</span> <span m='389220'>transactions</span>

  <span m='391080'>and</span> <span m='392040'>people</span> <span m='392280'>can</span>
  <span m='392430'>build</span> <span m='392610'>the</span> <span m='392700'>next</span>
  <span m='392940'>block.</span> </p><p><span m='394540'>So</span> <span m='395010'>the</span>

  <span m='396000'>the</span> <span m='396090'>current</span> <span m='396300'>problem</span>
  <span m='396660'>set</span> <span m='396840'>is</span> <span m='397080'>instead</span>
  <span m='397410'>of</span> <span m='397500'>putting</span> <span m='397740'>your</span>

  <span m='399210'>put--</span> <span m='400440'>you</span> <span m='400500'>can</span>
  <span m='400620'>put</span> <span m='400710'>your</span> <span m='400800'>name--</span>
  <span m='401050'>but</span> <span m='401190'>you</span> <span m='401340'>also</span>
  <span m='401640'>put</span> <span m='402120'>all</span> <span m='402480'>these</span>
  <span m='402720'>messages</span> <span m='403290'>that</span> <span m='403410'>you've</span>
  <span m='403560'>seen</span> <span m='403890'>recently.</span> <span m='404910'>And</span>
  <span m='405030'>so</span> <span m='405150'>you</span> <span m='405270'>commit</span>
  <span m='405540'>to</span> <span m='405660'>them</span> <span m='405840'>that</span>
  <span m='405990'>way.</span> </p><p><span m='407160'>You</span> <span m='407310'>could</span>
  <span m='407670'>do</span> <span m='407880'>it</span> <span m='408060'>by</span>
  <span m='408240'>just</span> <span m='408720'>sticking</span> <span m='409110'>them</span>
  <span m='409260'>all</span> <span m='409470'>in,</span> <span m='409930'>but</span>
  <span m='410760'>instead,</span> <span m='411600'>there's</span> <span m='411810'>a</span>
  <span m='411870'>bit</span> <span m='412320'>more</span> <span m='412740'>advanced</span>
  <span m='413160'>way</span> <span m='413280'>to</span> <span m='413370'>do</span>
  <span m='413490'>it.</span> <span m='414780'>You</span> <span m='415170'>use</span>
  <span m='415450'>what's</span> <span m='415590'>called</span> <span m='415770'>a</span>
  <span m='415830'>block</span> <span m='416160'>header.</span> <span m='417450'>So</span>
  <span m='417550'>yeah,</span> <span m='417750'>the</span> <span m='417850'>block</span>
  <span m='418050'>header</span> <span m='418440'>itself</span> <span m='418980'>is</span>
  <span m='419130'>the</span> <span m='419220'>message.</span> <span m='420420'>So</span>
  <span m='420690'>similar</span> <span m='421020'>to</span> <span m='421110'>the</span>
  <span m='421200'>problem</span> <span m='421470'>set,</span> <span m='422190'>it's</span>
  <span m='422340'>the</span> <span m='422400'>block</span> <span m='422670'>header</span>
  <span m='423090'>that</span> <span m='423210'>you</span> <span m='423300'>need</span>
  <span m='423450'>to</span> <span m='423540'>hash</span> <span m='423870'>to</span>
  <span m='423960'>get</span> <span m='424260'>a</span> <span m='424320'>low</span>
  <span m='424620'>output</span> <span m='424920'>value,</span> <span m='425730'>not</span>
  <span m='425970'>the</span> <span m='426120'>block</span> <span m='426480'>itself,</span>
  <span m='427330'>which</span> <span m='427490'>is</span> <span m='427560'>kind</span>
  <span m='427710'>of</span> <span m='427800'>interesting.</span> </p><p><span m='429040'>And</span>
  <span m='429300'>the</span> <span m='429360'>headers</span> <span m='429900'>have</span>

  <span m='431640'>all</span> <span m='431790'>the</span> <span m='431880'>transactions</span>

  <span m='432920'>So</span> <span m='433020'>you</span> <span m='433110'>don't</span>
  <span m='433260'>just</span> <span m='433410'>put</span> <span m='433560'>all</span>
  <span m='433650'>the</span> <span m='433740'>transactions</span> <span m='434730'>into</span>
  <span m='434940'>one</span> <span m='435120'>big</span> <span m='436080'>megabyte</span>
